Error: Usage: ttfautohint [OPTION]... [IN-FILE [OUT-FILE]]

Error: Replace hints in TrueType font IN-FILE and write output to OUT-FILE.

Error: If OUT-FILE is missing, standard output is used instead;

Error: if IN-FILE is missing also, standard input and output are used.

Error: 

Error: The new hints are based on FreeType's auto-hinter.

Error: 

Error: This program is a simple front-end to the `ttfautohint' library.

Error: 

Error: Long options can be given with one or two dashes,

Error: and with and without equal sign between option and argument.

Error: This means that the following forms are acceptable:

Error: `-foo=bar', `--foo=bar', `-foo bar', `--foo bar'.

Error: 

Error: Mandatory arguments to long options are mandatory for short options too.

Error: 

Error: Options:

Error:       --debug                print debugging information

Error:   -c, --composites           hint glyph composites also

Error:   -d, --dehint               remove all hints

Error:   -D, --default-script=S     set default OpenType script (default: latn)

Error:   -f, --fallback-script=S    set fallback script (default: none)

Error:   -G, --hinting-limit=N      switch off hinting above this PPEM value

Error:                              (default: 200); value 0 means no limit

Error:   -h, --help                 display this help and exit

Error:   -H, --fallback-stem-width=N

Error:                              set fallback stem width

Error:                              (default: 50 font units at 2048 UPEM)

Error:   -i, --ignore-restrictions  override font license restrictions

Error:   -l, --hinting-range-min=N  the minimum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 8)

Error:   -m, --deltas-file=FILE     get delta exceptions from FILE

Error:   -n, --no-info              don't add ttfautohint info

Error:                              to the version string(s) in the `name' table

Error:   -p, --adjust-subglyphs     handle subglyph adjustments in exotic fonts

Error:   -r, --hinting-range-max=N  the maximum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 50)

Error:   -s, --symbol               input is symbol font

Error:   -v, --verbose              show progress information

Error:   -V, --version              print version information and exit

Error:   -w, --strong-stem-width=S  use strong stem width routine for modes S,

Error:                              where S is a string of up to three letters

Error:                              with possible values `g' for grayscale,

Error:                              `G' for GDI ClearType, and `D' for

Error:                              DirectWrite ClearType (default: G)

Error:   -W, --windows-compatibility

Error:                              add blue zones for `usWinAscent' and

Error:                              `usWinDescent' to avoid clipping

Error:   -x, --increase-x-height=N  increase x height for sizes in the range

Error:                              6<=PPEM<=N; value 0 switches off this feature

Error:                              (default: 14)

Error:   -X, --x-height-snapping-exceptions=STRING

Error:                              specify a comma-separated list of

Error:                              x-height snapping exceptions, for example

Error:                              "-9, 13-17, 19" (default: "")

Error: 

Error: The program accepts both TTF and TTC files as input.

Error: Use option -i only if you have a legal permission to modify the font.

Error: The used PPEM value for option -p is FUnits per em, normally 2048.

Error: With option -s, use default values for standard stem width and height,

Error: otherwise they are derived from script-specific characters

Error: resembling the shape of character `o'.

Error: 

Error: A hint set contains the optimal hinting for a certain PPEM value;

Error: the larger the hint set range (as given by options -l and -r),

Error: the more hint sets get computed, usually increasing the output font size.

Error: The `gasp' table of the output file always enables grayscale hinting

Error: for all sizes (limited by option -G, which is handled in the bytecode).

Error: Increasing the value of -G does not increase the output font size.

Error: 

Error: Options -f and -D take a four-letter string that identifies a script.

Error: Option -f sets the script used as a fallback for glyphs that have

Error: character codes outside of known script ranges.  Option -D sets the

Error: default script for handling OpenType features.  Possible values are

Error: 

Error:   cyrl (Cyrillic),

Error:   deva (Devanagari),

Error:   grek (Greek),

Error:   hebr (Hebrew),

Error:   latn (Latin),

Error:   none (no script).

Error: 

Error: A delta exceptions file contains lines of the form

Error: 

Error:   [<subfont idx>] <glyph id> p <points> [x <shift>] [y <shift>] @ <ppems>

Error: 

Error: to fine-tune point positions after hinting.  <glyph id> is a glyph name

Error: or index, <shift> is in px, <points> and <ppems> are ranges as with

Error: option `-X'.  `#' starts a line comment, which gets ignored.

Error: Empty lines are ignored, too.

Error: 

Error: A GUI version of this program is called `ttfautohintGUI'.

Error: 

Error: Report bugs to: freetype-devel@nongnu.org

Error: ttfautohint home page: <http://www.freetype.org/ttfautohint>

Error: Usage: ttfautohint [OPTION]... [IN-FILE [OUT-FILE]]

Error: Replace hints in TrueType font IN-FILE and write output to OUT-FILE.

Error: If OUT-FILE is missing, standard output is used instead;

Error: if IN-FILE is missing also, standard input and output are used.

Error: 

Error: The new hints are based on FreeType's auto-hinter.

Error: 

Error: This program is a simple front-end to the `ttfautohint' library.

Error: 

Error: Long options can be given with one or two dashes,

Error: and with and without equal sign between option and argument.

Error: This means that the following forms are acceptable:

Error: `-foo=bar', `--foo=bar', `-foo bar', `--foo bar'.

Error: 

Error: Mandatory arguments to long options are mandatory for short options too.

Error: 

Error: Options:

Error:       --debug                print debugging information

Error:   -c, --composites           hint glyph composites also

Error:   -d, --dehint               remove all hints

Error:   -D, --default-script=S     set default OpenType script (default: latn)

Error:   -f, --fallback-script=S    set fallback script (default: none)

Error:   -G, --hinting-limit=N      switch off hinting above this PPEM value

Error:                              (default: 200); value 0 means no limit

Error:   -h, --help                 display this help and exit

Error:   -H, --fallback-stem-width=N

Error:                              set fallback stem width

Error:                              (default: 50 font units at 2048 UPEM)

Error:   -i, --ignore-restrictions  override font license restrictions

Error:   -l, --hinting-range-min=N  the minimum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 8)

Error:   -m, --deltas-file=FILE     get delta exceptions from FILE

Error:   -n, --no-info              don't add ttfautohint info

Error:                              to the version string(s) in the `name' table

Error:   -p, --adjust-subglyphs     handle subglyph adjustments in exotic fonts

Error:   -r, --hinting-range-max=N  the maximum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 50)

Error:   -s, --symbol               input is symbol font

Error:   -v, --verbose              show progress information

Error:   -V, --version              print version information and exit

Error:   -w, --strong-stem-width=S  use strong stem width routine for modes S,

Error:                              where S is a string of up to three letters

Error:                              with possible values `g' for grayscale,

Error:                              `G' for GDI ClearType, and `D' for

Error:                              DirectWrite ClearType (default: G)

Error:   -W, --windows-compatibility

Error:                              add blue zones for `usWinAscent' and

Error:                              `usWinDescent' to avoid clipping

Error:   -x, --increase-x-height=N  increase x height for sizes in the range

Error:                              6<=PPEM<=N; value 0 switches off this feature

Error:                              (default: 14)

Error:   -X, --x-height-snapping-exceptions=STRING

Error:                              specify a comma-separated list of

Error:                              x-height snapping exceptions, for example

Error:                              "-9, 13-17, 19" (default: "")

Error: 

Error: The program accepts both TTF and TTC files as input.

Error: Use option -i only if you have a legal permission to modify the font.

Error: The used PPEM value for option -p is FUnits per em, normally 2048.

Error: With option -s, use default values for standard stem width and height,

Error: otherwise they are derived from script-specific characters

Error: resembling the shape of character `o'.

Error: 

Error: A hint set contains the optimal hinting for a certain PPEM value;

Error: the larger the hint set range (as given by options -l and -r),

Error: the more hint sets get computed, usually increasing the output font size.

Error: The `gasp' table of the output file always enables grayscale hinting

Error: for all sizes (limited by option -G, which is handled in the bytecode).

Error: Increasing the value of -G does not increase the output font size.

Error: 

Error: Options -f and -D take a four-letter string that identifies a script.

Error: Option -f sets the script used as a fallback for glyphs that have

Error: character codes outside of known script ranges.  Option -D sets the

Error: default script for handling OpenType features.  Possible values are

Error: 

Error:   cyrl (Cyrillic),

Error:   deva (Devanagari),

Error:   grek (Greek),

Error:   hebr (Hebrew),

Error:   latn (Latin),

Error:   none (no script).

Error: 

Error: A delta exceptions file contains lines of the form

Error: 

Error:   [<subfont idx>] <glyph id> p <points> [x <shift>] [y <shift>] @ <ppems>

Error: 

Error: to fine-tune point positions after hinting.  <glyph id> is a glyph name

Error: or index, <shift> is in px, <points> and <ppems> are ranges as with

Error: option `-X'.  `#' starts a line comment, which gets ignored.

Error: Empty lines are ignored, too.

Error: 

Error: A GUI version of this program is called `ttfautohintGUI'.

Error: 

Error: Report bugs to: freetype-devel@nongnu.org

Error: ttfautohint home page: <http://www.freetype.org/ttfautohint>

Error: Usage: ttfautohint [OPTION]... [IN-FILE [OUT-FILE]]

Error: Replace hints in TrueType font IN-FILE and write output to OUT-FILE.

Error: If OUT-FILE is missing, standard output is used instead;

Error: if IN-FILE is missing also, standard input and output are used.

Error: 

Error: The new hints are based on FreeType's auto-hinter.

Error: 

Error: This program is a simple front-end to the `ttfautohint' library.

Error: 

Error: Long options can be given with one or two dashes,

Error: and with and without equal sign between option and argument.

Error: This means that the following forms are acceptable:

Error: `-foo=bar', `--foo=bar', `-foo bar', `--foo bar'.

Error: 

Error: Mandatory arguments to long options are mandatory for short options too.

Error: 

Error: Options:

Error:       --debug                print debugging information

Error:   -c, --composites           hint glyph composites also

Error:   -d, --dehint               remove all hints

Error:   -D, --default-script=S     set default OpenType script (default: latn)

Error:   -f, --fallback-script=S    set fallback script (default: none)

Error:   -G, --hinting-limit=N      switch off hinting above this PPEM value

Error:                              (default: 200); value 0 means no limit

Error:   -h, --help                 display this help and exit

Error:   -H, --fallback-stem-width=N

Error:                              set fallback stem width

Error:                              (default: 50 font units at 2048 UPEM)

Error:   -i, --ignore-restrictions  override font license restrictions

Error:   -l, --hinting-range-min=N  the minimum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 8)

Error:   -m, --deltas-file=FILE     get delta exceptions from FILE

Error:   -n, --no-info              don't add ttfautohint info

Error:                              to the version string(s) in the `name' table

Error:   -p, --adjust-subglyphs     handle subglyph adjustments in exotic fonts

Error:   -r, --hinting-range-max=N  the maximum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 50)

Error:   -s, --symbol               input is symbol font

Error:   -v, --verbose              show progress information

Error:   -V, --version              print version information and exit

Error:   -w, --strong-stem-width=S  use strong stem width routine for modes S,

Error:                              where S is a string of up to three letters

Error:                              with possible values `g' for grayscale,

Error:                              `G' for GDI ClearType, and `D' for

Error:                              DirectWrite ClearType (default: G)

Error:   -W, --windows-compatibility

Error:                              add blue zones for `usWinAscent' and

Error:                              `usWinDescent' to avoid clipping

Error:   -x, --increase-x-height=N  increase x height for sizes in the range

Error:                              6<=PPEM<=N; value 0 switches off this feature

Error:                              (default: 14)

Error:   -X, --x-height-snapping-exceptions=STRING

Error:                              specify a comma-separated list of

Error:                              x-height snapping exceptions, for example

Error:                              "-9, 13-17, 19" (default: "")

Error: 

Error: The program accepts both TTF and TTC files as input.

Error: Use option -i only if you have a legal permission to modify the font.

Error: The used PPEM value for option -p is FUnits per em, normally 2048.

Error: With option -s, use default values for standard stem width and height,

Error: otherwise they are derived from script-specific characters

Error: resembling the shape of character `o'.

Error: 

Error: A hint set contains the optimal hinting for a certain PPEM value;

Error: the larger the hint set range (as given by options -l and -r),

Error: the more hint sets get computed, usually increasing the output font size.

Error: The `gasp' table of the output file always enables grayscale hinting

Error: for all sizes (limited by option -G, which is handled in the bytecode).

Error: Increasing the value of -G does not increase the output font size.

Error: 

Error: Options -f and -D take a four-letter string that identifies a script.

Error: Option -f sets the script used as a fallback for glyphs that have

Error: character codes outside of known script ranges.  Option -D sets the

Error: default script for handling OpenType features.  Possible values are

Error: 

Error:   cyrl (Cyrillic),

Error:   deva (Devanagari),

Error:   grek (Greek),

Error:   hebr (Hebrew),

Error:   latn (Latin),

Error:   none (no script).

Error: 

Error: A delta exceptions file contains lines of the form

Error: 

Error:   [<subfont idx>] <glyph id> p <points> [x <shift>] [y <shift>] @ <ppems>

Error: 

Error: to fine-tune point positions after hinting.  <glyph id> is a glyph name

Error: or index, <shift> is in px, <points> and <ppems> are ranges as with

Error: option `-X'.  `#' starts a line comment, which gets ignored.

Error: Empty lines are ignored, too.

Error: 

Error: A GUI version of this program is called `ttfautohintGUI'.

Error: 

Error: Report bugs to: freetype-devel@nongnu.org

Error: ttfautohint home page: <http://www.freetype.org/ttfautohint>

Error: Usage: ttfautohint [OPTION]... [IN-FILE [OUT-FILE]]

Error: Replace hints in TrueType font IN-FILE and write output to OUT-FILE.

Error: If OUT-FILE is missing, standard output is used instead;

Error: if IN-FILE is missing also, standard input and output are used.

Error: 

Error: The new hints are based on FreeType's auto-hinter.

Error: 

Error: This program is a simple front-end to the `ttfautohint' library.

Error: 

Error: Long options can be given with one or two dashes,

Error: and with and without equal sign between option and argument.

Error: This means that the following forms are acceptable:

Error: `-foo=bar', `--foo=bar', `-foo bar', `--foo bar'.

Error: 

Error: Mandatory arguments to long options are mandatory for short options too.

Error: 

Error: Options:

Error:       --debug                print debugging information

Error:   -c, --composites           hint glyph composites also

Error:   -d, --dehint               remove all hints

Error:   -D, --default-script=S     set default OpenType script (default: latn)

Error:   -f, --fallback-script=S    set fallback script (default: none)

Error:   -G, --hinting-limit=N      switch off hinting above this PPEM value

Error:                              (default: 200); value 0 means no limit

Error:   -h, --help                 display this help and exit

Error:   -H, --fallback-stem-width=N

Error:                              set fallback stem width

Error:                              (default: 50 font units at 2048 UPEM)

Error:   -i, --ignore-restrictions  override font license restrictions

Error:   -l, --hinting-range-min=N  the minimum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 8)

Error:   -m, --deltas-file=FILE     get delta exceptions from FILE

Error:   -n, --no-info              don't add ttfautohint info

Error:                              to the version string(s) in the `name' table

Error:   -p, --adjust-subglyphs     handle subglyph adjustments in exotic fonts

Error:   -r, --hinting-range-max=N  the maximum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 50)

Error:   -s, --symbol               input is symbol font

Error:   -v, --verbose              show progress information

Error:   -V, --version              print version information and exit

Error:   -w, --strong-stem-width=S  use strong stem width routine for modes S,

Error:                              where S is a string of up to three letters

Error:                              with possible values `g' for grayscale,

Error:                              `G' for GDI ClearType, and `D' for

Error:                              DirectWrite ClearType (default: G)

Error:   -W, --windows-compatibility

Error:                              add blue zones for `usWinAscent' and

Error:                              `usWinDescent' to avoid clipping

Error:   -x, --increase-x-height=N  increase x height for sizes in the range

Error:                              6<=PPEM<=N; value 0 switches off this feature

Error:                              (default: 14)

Error:   -X, --x-height-snapping-exceptions=STRING

Error:                              specify a comma-separated list of

Error:                              x-height snapping exceptions, for example

Error:                              "-9, 13-17, 19" (default: "")

Error: 

Error: The program accepts both TTF and TTC files as input.

Error: Use option -i only if you have a legal permission to modify the font.

Error: The used PPEM value for option -p is FUnits per em, normally 2048.

Error: With option -s, use default values for standard stem width and height,

Error: otherwise they are derived from script-specific characters

Error: resembling the shape of character `o'.

Error: 

Error: A hint set contains the optimal hinting for a certain PPEM value;

Error: the larger the hint set range (as given by options -l and -r),

Error: the more hint sets get computed, usually increasing the output font size.

Error: The `gasp' table of the output file always enables grayscale hinting

Error: for all sizes (limited by option -G, which is handled in the bytecode).

Error: Increasing the value of -G does not increase the output font size.

Error: 

Error: Options -f and -D take a four-letter string that identifies a script.

Error: Option -f sets the script used as a fallback for glyphs that have

Error: character codes outside of known script ranges.  Option -D sets the

Error: default script for handling OpenType features.  Possible values are

Error: 

Error:   cyrl (Cyrillic),

Error:   deva (Devanagari),

Error:   grek (Greek),

Error:   hebr (Hebrew),

Error:   latn (Latin),

Error:   none (no script).

Error: 

Error: A delta exceptions file contains lines of the form

Error: 

Error:   [<subfont idx>] <glyph id> p <points> [x <shift>] [y <shift>] @ <ppems>

Error: 

Error: to fine-tune point positions after hinting.  <glyph id> is a glyph name

Error: or index, <shift> is in px, <points> and <ppems> are ranges as with

Error: option `-X'.  `#' starts a line comment, which gets ignored.

Error: Empty lines are ignored, too.

Error: 

Error: A GUI version of this program is called `ttfautohintGUI'.

Error: 

Error: Report bugs to: freetype-devel@nongnu.org

Error: ttfautohint home page: <http://www.freetype.org/ttfautohint>

Error: Usage: ttfautohint [OPTION]... [IN-FILE [OUT-FILE]]

Error: Replace hints in TrueType font IN-FILE and write output to OUT-FILE.

Error: If OUT-FILE is missing, standard output is used instead;

Error: if IN-FILE is missing also, standard input and output are used.

Error: 

Error: The new hints are based on FreeType's auto-hinter.

Error: 

Error: This program is a simple front-end to the `ttfautohint' library.

Error: 

Error: Long options can be given with one or two dashes,

Error: and with and without equal sign between option and argument.

Error: This means that the following forms are acceptable:

Error: `-foo=bar', `--foo=bar', `-foo bar', `--foo bar'.

Error: 

Error: Mandatory arguments to long options are mandatory for short options too.

Error: 

Error: Options:

Error:       --debug                print debugging information

Error:   -c, --composites           hint glyph composites also

Error:   -d, --dehint               remove all hints

Error:   -D, --default-script=S     set default OpenType script (default: latn)

Error:   -f, --fallback-script=S    set fallback script (default: none)

Error:   -G, --hinting-limit=N      switch off hinting above this PPEM value

Error:                              (default: 200); value 0 means no limit

Error:   -h, --help                 display this help and exit

Error:   -H, --fallback-stem-width=N

Error:                              set fallback stem width

Error:                              (default: 50 font units at 2048 UPEM)

Error:   -i, --ignore-restrictions  override font license restrictions

Error:   -l, --hinting-range-min=N  the minimum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 8)

Error:   -m, --deltas-file=FILE     get delta exceptions from FILE

Error:   -n, --no-info              don't add ttfautohint info

Error:                              to the version string(s) in the `name' table

Error:   -p, --adjust-subglyphs     handle subglyph adjustments in exotic fonts

Error:   -r, --hinting-range-max=N  the maximum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 50)

Error:   -s, --symbol               input is symbol font

Error:   -v, --verbose              show progress information

Error:   -V, --version              print version information and exit

Error:   -w, --strong-stem-width=S  use strong stem width routine for modes S,

Error:                              where S is a string of up to three letters

Error:                              with possible values `g' for grayscale,

Error:                              `G' for GDI ClearType, and `D' for

Error:                              DirectWrite ClearType (default: G)

Error:   -W, --windows-compatibility

Error:                              add blue zones for `usWinAscent' and

Error:                              `usWinDescent' to avoid clipping

Error:   -x, --increase-x-height=N  increase x height for sizes in the range

Error:                              6<=PPEM<=N; value 0 switches off this feature

Error:                              (default: 14)

Error:   -X, --x-height-snapping-exceptions=STRING

Error:                              specify a comma-separated list of

Error:                              x-height snapping exceptions, for example

Error:                              "-9, 13-17, 19" (default: "")

Error: 

Error: The program accepts both TTF and TTC files as input.

Error: Use option -i only if you have a legal permission to modify the font.

Error: The used PPEM value for option -p is FUnits per em, normally 2048.

Error: With option -s, use default values for standard stem width and height,

Error: otherwise they are derived from script-specific characters

Error: resembling the shape of character `o'.

Error: 

Error: A hint set contains the optimal hinting for a certain PPEM value;

Error: the larger the hint set range (as given by options -l and -r),

Error: the more hint sets get computed, usually increasing the output font size.

Error: The `gasp' table of the output file always enables grayscale hinting

Error: for all sizes (limited by option -G, which is handled in the bytecode).

Error: Increasing the value of -G does not increase the output font size.

Error: 

Error: Options -f and -D take a four-letter string that identifies a script.

Error: Option -f sets the script used as a fallback for glyphs that have

Error: character codes outside of known script ranges.  Option -D sets the

Error: default script for handling OpenType features.  Possible values are

Error: 

Error:   cyrl (Cyrillic),

Error:   deva (Devanagari),

Error:   grek (Greek),

Error:   hebr (Hebrew),

Error:   latn (Latin),

Error:   none (no script).

Error: 

Error: A delta exceptions file contains lines of the form

Error: 

Error:   [<subfont idx>] <glyph id> p <points> [x <shift>] [y <shift>] @ <ppems>

Error: 

Error: to fine-tune point positions after hinting.  <glyph id> is a glyph name

Error: or index, <shift> is in px, <points> and <ppems> are ranges as with

Error: option `-X'.  `#' starts a line comment, which gets ignored.

Error: Empty lines are ignored, too.

Error: 

Error: A GUI version of this program is called `ttfautohintGUI'.

Error: 

Error: Report bugs to: freetype-devel@nongnu.org

Error: ttfautohint home page: <http://www.freetype.org/ttfautohint>

### Autohint TTFs (ttfautohint) Playfair Display-Regular Italic.ttf
$ ttfautohint -l 7 -r 28 -G 50 -x 13 -w "G" /home/travis/build/fontdirectory/playfairdisplay/builds/build/Playfair Display-Regular Italic.ttf '/home/travis/build/fontdirectory/playfairdisplay/builds/build/Playfair Display-Regular Italic.autohint.ttf'

Error: Usage: ttfautohint [OPTION]... [IN-FILE [OUT-FILE]]

Error: Replace hints in TrueType font IN-FILE and write output to OUT-FILE.

Error: If OUT-FILE is missing, standard output is used instead;

Error: if IN-FILE is missing also, standard input and output are used.

Error: 

Error: The new hints are based on FreeType's auto-hinter.

Error: 

Error: This program is a simple front-end to the `ttfautohint' library.

Error: 

Error: Long options can be given with one or two dashes,

Error: and with and without equal sign between option and argument.

Error: This means that the following forms are acceptable:

Error: `-foo=bar', `--foo=bar', `-foo bar', `--foo bar'.

Error: 

Error: Mandatory arguments to long options are mandatory for short options too.

Error: 

Error: Options:

Error:       --debug                print debugging information

Error:   -c, --composites           hint glyph composites also

Error:   -d, --dehint               remove all hints

Error:   -D, --default-script=S     set default OpenType script (default: latn)

Error:   -f, --fallback-script=S    set fallback script (default: none)

Error:   -G, --hinting-limit=N      switch off hinting above this PPEM value

Error:                              (default: 200); value 0 means no limit

Error:   -h, --help                 display this help and exit

Error:   -H, --fallback-stem-width=N

Error:                              set fallback stem width

Error:                              (default: 50 font units at 2048 UPEM)

Error:   -i, --ignore-restrictions  override font license restrictions

Error:   -l, --hinting-range-min=N  the minimum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 8)

Error:   -m, --deltas-file=FILE     get delta exceptions from FILE

Error:   -n, --no-info              don't add ttfautohint info

Error:                              to the version string(s) in the `name' table

Error:   -p, --adjust-subglyphs     handle subglyph adjustments in exotic fonts

Error:   -r, --hinting-range-max=N  the maximum PPEM value for hint sets

Error:                              (default: 50)

Error:   -s, --symbol               input is symbol font

Error:   -v, --verbose              show progress information

Error:   -V, --version              print version information and exit

Error:   -w, --strong-stem-width=S  use strong stem width routine for modes S,

Error:                              where S is a string of up to three letters

Error:                              with possible values `g' for grayscale,

Error:                              `G' for GDI ClearType, and `D' for

Error:                              DirectWrite ClearType (default: G)

Error:   -W, --windows-compatibility

Error:                              add blue zones for `usWinAscent' and

Error:                              `usWinDescent' to avoid clipping

Error:   -x, --increase-x-height=N  increase x height for sizes in the range

Error:                              6<=PPEM<=N; value 0 switches off this feature

Error:                              (default: 14)

Error:   -X, --x-height-snapping-exceptions=STRING

Error:                              specify a comma-separated list of

Error:                              x-height snapping exceptions, for example

Error:                              "-9, 13-17, 19" (default: "")

Error: 

Error: The program accepts both TTF and TTC files as input.

Error: Use option -i only if you have a legal permission to modify the font.

Error: The used PPEM value for option -p is FUnits per em, normally 2048.

Error: With option -s, use default values for standard stem width and height,

Error: otherwise they are derived from script-specific characters

Error: resembling the shape of character `o'.

Error: 

Error: A hint set contains the optimal hinting for a certain PPEM value;

Error: the larger the hint set range (as given by options -l and -r),

Error: the more hint sets get computed, usually increasing the output font size.

Error: The `gasp' table of the output file always enables grayscale hinting

Error: for all sizes (limited by option -G, which is handled in the bytecode).

Error: Increasing the value of -G does not increase the output font size.

Error: 

Error: Options -f and -D take a four-letter string that identifies a script.

Error: Option -f sets the script used as a fallback for glyphs that have

Error: character codes outside of known script ranges.  Option -D sets the

Error: default script for handling OpenType features.  Possible values are

Error: 

Error:   cyrl (Cyrillic),

Error:   deva (Devanagari),

Error:   grek (Greek),

Error:   hebr (Hebrew),

Error:   latn (Latin),

Error:   none (no script).

Error: 

Error: A delta exceptions file contains lines of the form

Error: 

Error:   [<subfont idx>] <glyph id> p <points> [x <shift>] [y <shift>] @ <ppems>

Error: 

Error: to fine-tune point positions after hinting.  <glyph id> is a glyph name

Error: or index, <shift> is in px, <points> and <ppems> are ranges as with

Error: option `-X'.  `#' starts a line comment, which gets ignored.

Error: Empty lines are ignored, too.

Error: 

Error: A GUI version of this program is called `ttfautohintGUI'.

Error: 

Error: Report bugs to: freetype-devel@nongnu.org

Error: ttfautohint home page: <http://www.freetype.org/ttfautohint>
